</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">despicable</span>,  <span class="Latn" lang="en">reprehensible</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">inferior</span>,  <span class="Latn" lang="en">lesser</span></li></ol>

***vuil.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vuil.html>vuil</a> (2430)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vuul</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fūl</i>. The adjective <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fūlaz</i>, the noun from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fūlą</i>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pū-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pew-</i>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">foul</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">faul</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">ful</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuil.html>vuil</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuiler.html>vuiler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">vuilst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dirty, filthy</li>
<li>obscene, lewd</li>
<li>dishonorable</li>
<li>illegal, improper</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fouled, having its wetted surface polluted by marine organisms</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="3" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervuilen.html>vervuilen</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuilnis.html>vuilnis</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">vuilte</span></li></ul></div><div class="list-switcher-element" data-showtext=" show more ▼ " data-hidetext=" show less  " style="display: none;"> </div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuil.html>vuil</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuil.html>vuiltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dirt, filth</li>
<li>garbage, trash, waste, litter</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vuil.html>vuil</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schoon.html>schoon</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bevuilen.html>bevuild</a></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>viezigheid, <a href = vnd.unilang:onrein.html>onreine</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:materie.html>materie</a></li></ol>

***vuilnis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vuilnis.html>vuilnis</a> (5159)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuil.html>vuil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dirty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuilnis.html>vuilnis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>rubbish, trash, garbage; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">especially</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> waste products (to be) disposed off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vuilnis.html>vuilnis</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:overal.html>overal</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">There <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>trash</b> everywhere.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***vulgaris.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a> (86278)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vulgus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the multitude, the masses</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-āris</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la">vulgāris</strong> (<i>neuter</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">vulgāre</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">vulgārissimus</b>, <i>adverb</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">vulgāre</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">vulgāriter</b>); <i>third-declension two-termination adjective</i>
</p>
<ol><li>common, usual, commonly known</li>
<li>simple, plain</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>In New Latin, within taxonomic binomial nomenclature, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a specific epithet in many genera, across all kingdoms, denoting a common (prevalent) species of the genus (for example, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beta_vulgaris" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Beta vulgaris">Beta <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vespula_vulgaris" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Vespula vulgaris">Vespula <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/common_starling" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:common starling">Sturnus <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></a></i>), and within disease classification and nomenclature (nosology), it denotes the common or classic form of any of various disorders (for example, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/acne" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:acne">acne <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/impetigo" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:impetigo">impetigo <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/psoriasis" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:psoriasis">psoriasis <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></a>). Thus, because the word <a href = vnd.unilang:labels.html>labels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> that are common and widespread, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> itself common and widespread (a trait it shares with the <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">common</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">regular</i>, and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">classic</i>). 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="la">vulgāritās</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="la">vulgāriter</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="la">vulgārius</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="la">vulgātē</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="la">vulgātor</span></li></ul>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="la">vulgātus</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="la">vulgivagus</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="la">vulgō</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="la">vulgus</span></li></ul>
</div>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuren.html>vuren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to set on fire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fiuron</i>. ***vuur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vuur.html>vuur</a> (791)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuur.html>vuur</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fuir</i>, from West-Germanic *<i>fuïr-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fōr</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*péh₂wr̥</i>. The adjectival <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a calque of the <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> sense of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fire</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuur.html>vuur</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuren.html>vuren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuurtje.html>vuurtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fire
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vuur.html>vuur</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:brandde.html>brandde</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koud.html>koud</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>fire</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> burning in my room; it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> cold.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>heater</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a lighter
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>Heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vuur.html>vuur</a></b>?</i>
<dl><dd>Got a <b>light</b>?</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>The act of firing with firearms, explosives or less commonly other projectile <a href = vnd.unilang:weapons.html>weapons</a>; fire.</li></ol>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuur.html>vuur</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vlieg.html>vlieg</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuurvlieg.html>vuurvlieg</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuurvliegen.html>vuurvliegen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuurvliegje.html>vuurvliegje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A firefly, beetle of the family Lampyridae, especially its <a href = vnd.unilang:grub.html>grub</a>.</li></ol>

***waag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:waag.html>waag</a> (3001)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wâge</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wāga</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wēgō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waag.html>waag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wagen.html>wagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waagje.html>waagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>weighing scales
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weegschaal.html>weegschaal</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>place (building) where goods are weighed
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">waaggebouw</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">boterwaag</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">heksenwaag</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kaaswaag</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waagschaal.html>waagschaal</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wāge</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>, alternative form of <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">waech</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wāg</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wēgaz</i>. The feminine may be a <a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>mere</a> variant (if old from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wāga</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wēgō</i>), or it may be due to a merger with another word with an original short vowel, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> attested in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:wagen.html>wage</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">movement, shaking</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">waga</i>. See <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wegen.html>Woge</a></i> for more.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waag.html>waag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wagen.html>wagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waagje.html>waagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>wave</li>
<li>water flow, current</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>

***waaien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:waaien.html>waaien</a> (14185)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wâyen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wāien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wēaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂weh₁-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waaien.html>waaien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of the wind</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blow
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote?)</span>  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:johannes.html>Johannes</a> 3:8</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.biblija.net/biblija.cgi?m=Johannes+3amp;id18=1amp;pos=0amp;l=nlamp;set=10">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> wind <b><a href = vnd.unilang:waait.html>waait</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarheen.html>waarheen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoort.html>hoort</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geluid.html>geluid</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaan.html>vandaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>Zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iedereen.html>iedereen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geest.html>Geest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geboren.html>geboren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The wind <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blows.html>blows</a></b> where it wants; you hear its sound, but you don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> know where it <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> from and where it goes to. So it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> with everyone that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> born out of the Spirit.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of the weather</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be windy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:waaide.html>waaide</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> hard.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It <b><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a></b> very <b>windy</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***waar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> (53)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wāer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*war</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwar</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">where</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> where, in which place
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>Waar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Jan?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Where</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> John?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> where, the place that
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woont.html>woont</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>where</b> he <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with a preposition</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> what, which thing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>Waar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>What</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that good for?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with a preposition</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> what, that which
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>what</b> that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> good for.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>With a preposition, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used instead of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></i> to create a pronominal adverb. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>See Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wâer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wār</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wēraz</i>.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wāre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wara</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*warō</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ware.html>ware</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:waaraan.html>waaraan</a> (3777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wāert</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wēert</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wert</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*werduz</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-vries_tollenaere_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-vries_tollenaere-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waard.html>waard</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waarden.html>waarden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waard.html>waardje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">waardin</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>innkeeper, publican
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herbergier.html>herbergier</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kastelein.html>kastelein</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms hyponym"><span class="defdate">Hyponym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">waardin</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>landlord, host</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The master of the household; a husband</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A protector, lord</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wert</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wāert</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">werth</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*werþaz</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-vries_tollenaere_1-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-vries_tollenaere-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waard.html>waard</a></strong> (<i>used only predicatively</i>, <i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">following a noun phrase</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> worth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:waard.html>waard</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That money <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>worth</b> nothing.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wāert</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wēert</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wert</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*werith</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*wariþ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wariþa-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*waruþa-</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-vries_tollenaere_1-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-vries_tollenaere-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waard.html>waard</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waarden.html>waarden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waard.html>waardje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>holm, holme, area surrounded by rivers</li>
<li>type of foreland, outside a local system of dikes</li>
<li>dwelling mound
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">terp</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waarde.html>waarde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waarden.html>waarden</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">waardes</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waarde.html>waardetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">waerdi</i>, a contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">waert gi</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waart.html>waart</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>).
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The contraction <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes reinforced with an additional <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>, giving <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waarde.html>waarde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">waernēmen</i>.
